 is final mukaable main pehla gol bharat ne kiya

 nirdhaarit samay kaa khel samaapt hone tak donon timen 2-2 kii barabari par rahi

 is dauraan camerun team ne aakraamak rukh akhriyaar karte hue ek ke baad ek hamale kiye lekin bhartiya rakshapankti ne in hamalon ko naakaam kar diya

 muqabla penalty shoot out main pahunchaa

 mujhe to bura lag rahaa he kisi kaa number is tarah se public main discus kiya ja rahaa he, wo bhi pradhanmantri kaa
 Yet the Aam Aadmi Party is aggressive
 ashutosh ne amit shah or arun jetali ko nyauta diya he ki ve bhi saath chalem dilli vishvavidhyalay
 The two will examine the papers together
 4 may ko aam aadmi party kii taraf se ashutosh, ashish khetaan or raghav chaddha dilli vishvavidhyalay gaye the
 He had the letter of authority of Mukhyamantri Kejriwal, in which the Central Information Commission had ordered information about PM Modi's degree to Kejriwal
 mukhyamantri kejariwal ne apana adhikaar in teen netaaon ko hastantarit kar diya tha
 All three stayed there for an hour
 baahar aakar kaha ki hamen koi jaankaree nahin di gai
 Take information from PMO
 'aap' ke netaa mangalvaar ko phir se dilli vishvavidhyalay jaayenge
 Chief Minister Kejriwal has tweeted that the documents have been sealed in Delhi University
 bijepi ne press conference main farzi dastauez pesh kiye hai
 The order of the Central Information Commissioner should be implemented and it should be allowed to investigate
 kaayade se dilli vishvavidhyalay ko hi ab tak jaankaree dekar is vivaad ko rafa-dfa kar dena chahie tha jaisaa ki gujarat vishvavidhyalay ne kiya
 Gujarat University issued his degree and stated that 1983 passed the first class MA
 ab ek sawaal uthaaya ja rahaa he ki pradhanmantri kii degree par antair polytical science likhaa he
 The leader of the Aam Aadmi Party says that he has never seen or heard the degree of political politics
 hamaare sahyogi rajeev pathak ne bataaya he ki gujarat main pehle sampurna rajyashastra kii degree milti thi
 Political science in Gujarati is called state science
 hindi pradeshon main raajnneeti shaastra kehete hai
 Thankfully no one has said that political science has heard what state science is
 varna or funs jate
 You must have understood the issue of anti-political science
 agar aapane polytical science ke saath koi sabsidyari vishay na padhaa ho to aisi degree milti thi
 On reading all the papers of the same subject, the degree of complete state science was obtained
 kejariwal ne na sirf is masale ko uthaaya balki duusare dalon par bhi dabaav uthaaya ki wo kyon nahin bol rahe hai
 The Congress came into effect and talked about the degree, but Bihar Chief Minister Nitish Kumar distanced himself from the controversy
 darasal degree or naam ke vivaad kaa khel sabane khelaa he
 In 2005 Subramanian Swamy went to the Supreme Court asking the Election Commission to file a complaint against Sonia Gandhi
 swami ke anusaar sonia gandhi ne 2004 ke halafname main apni degree ke bare main galat jaankaree di thi
 According to the Hindu newspaper report of 12 April 2005, when Dr
 Swamy asked Cambridge University about Sonia Gandhi's degree, she was told that she had never been a student
 swami ne yah bhi aarope lagaaya tha ki sonia ne angrezi main jis certificate course kaa zikr kiya he, wo cambridge ke kisi bhi english teaching shop se mil saktaa he
 The Supreme Court dismissed Swamy's petition
 supreme court ne kaha ki jab sonia gandhi ne koi jaankaree chhipaai nahin, tab kis baat ke liye aadesh den
 Swamy was not in the BJP then
 janata party ke netaa the
 Swamy is now in the BJP and has become a member of the Rajya Sabha
 swami ne supreme court ke aadesh ke baad bhi is masale ko kai baar uthaaya he
 According to the One India website, on the day of July 14, 2015, Swamy raised a case of Sonia's degree in Bangalore, which has a video available on youtube
 swami kaa kahana tha ki sonia gandhi sirf paanchavin class tak padhi hai
 Sonia Gandhi has said in her affidavit that she has a phd from Cambridge University
 lekin main sabit kar saktaa hum ki unki degree nakli he
 Sonia Gandhi can also go to jail like Aam Aadmi Party leader Jitendra Singh Tomar
 somvaar ko bijepi ke rashtriya adhyaksh amit shah ne kaha ki kejariwal ne saarvajanik jivan ke str ko giraaya he
 Swami has also spoken of sending Sonia Gandhi to jail like Tomar
 kya swami ne bhi kejariwal kii tarah saarvajanik jivan ke str ko giraaya he
 Meanwhile, the news has come that the membership of Madhya Pradesh BJP MLA Moti Kashyap has come to an end
 moti kashyap katni kii badvaara seat se vidhayak rahe hai or mantri bhi rahane kaa mauka mila he
 The Supreme Court has found Moti Kashyap's caste certificate to be fake
 ve 2008 main bhi vidhayak chune gaye the
 The Supreme Court has declared his election as void
 vah 2013 main bhi chune gaye jisaki sadsyta khatare main bataai ja rahi he
 Fraudulent actions can also be started on them
 2013 main jabalpur hoicourt ne unke 2008 ke vidhayak chune jane ko khaarij kar diya tha
 The Jabalpur High Court, while hearing the petition of Ramlal Keel, a tribal leader from Barwara, had found that Moti Kashyap described himself as a Scheduled Tribe and won the election from the reserve seat
 adaalat ne paaya ki kashyap anusuchit janajati ke nahin balki dhimar jati ke hai, jo obisi main aati he
 The comments somvaar ko ek or khabar ai ki maharashtra ke kolhapur kii meyar ashvini ramane kaa pad radd ho chukaa he
 She is no longer the mayor
 ensipi kii ashvini ramane ne farzi jati praaanpatr dekar parshad kaa chunaav ladaa tha
 a case of two birth certificates is also found along with fake degrees
 purv senadhyaksh or maujuuda kendriya mantri wike singh ke to do-do janm pramaan patr nikal aae
 There was so much controversy
 logon ke certificate main or ghar main janmdin kii tareekhen alag ho jaati hai
 Own country is wonder isliye aap degree vivaad ko hameshaa halke main nahin le sakate
 Making fake certificates is also a fact in our country
 farzi degree kii dukaane bhi khuli hai, yah bhi normal he
 The tenth fell will get the twelfth pass
 bhartiya reserve bank ke garvanar raghuram rajan ne shivanadar vishvavidhyalay ke dikshant samaaroh main bolte hue kaha ki chaatro ko shiksha ke liye karz lete vakt saavdhaanee baratani chahie
 They should avoid schools that put them in deep debt in the name of a useless degree
 rajan ne kaha ki hamen dekhnaa chahie ki beimaan skool aise chaatro ko nishaanaa na banaaen jinhen unke bare main pataa nahin he, kyonki aise main wo bekaar kii degree ke saath-saath karz main funs jate hai
 Sometimes your degree is correct, but college is fake
 kai baar kalege sahi hota he magar uski degree farji kii tarah nikal aati he
 Recently our colleague Srinivasan Jain did a story from Punjab
 medical college main doctor hai nahin, magar manyata mil chuki he
 How many engineering colleges are running like this
 aise sansthaanon main lakhon chaatr fanse rahete hai or fees bhar bharkar apni asli degree le lete hai
 At times, there are also reports that the accrediting institutions distributed the money with recognition
 isliye degree or bhagwaan donon ke bare main pataa karnaa itnaa aasaan nahin he apane yahaan
 When the question was raised on the degree of former Delhi Law Minister Jitendra Singh Tomar, how much was the police shown
 kai rajyon kaa daura kiya
 Tomar was arrested and he had to resign from the post
 aapako yaad dilaa den tab mukhyamantri kejariwal ne tomars kaa bachaav kiya tha, magar jab adaalat main tomars apni begunaahi sabit nahin kar paae to istipha lenaa padaa
 At that time, questions were raised about the degree of many leaders, but in their case, Tomar-like readiness was not shown
 zaahir he aam aadmi party or mukhyamantri kejariwal pradhanmantri kii degree kaa maamla uthaakar vaise hi aakraamak ho rahe the, jaise unhen dilli police tomars ke maamle main sakriy lagati thi
 The leaders of the Aam Aadmi Party were actively tweeting
 chunauti de rahe the or apni degree bataakar pradhanmantri kii degree puch rahe the
 The case got formal recognition when the Central Information Commissioner on 29 April directed the PMO and Delhi University to provide information about the Prime Minister's degree
 dilli vishvavidhyalay or piemo ne degree ke maamle main koi jaankaree di he yaa nahin, mujhe nahin pataa
 But on Monday, BJP National President Amit Shah and Finance Minister Arun Jaitley held a press conference and released the Prime Minister's BA and MA degrees
 bijepi bhi kya karti
 So many questions were arising that had to be answered, but if Delhi University had answered on its behalf, then these two important persons would not have to waste their time for this subject
 somvaar ko dopaher 1 baje bulaai gai press conference main amit shah or arun jetali ne pradhanmantri kii degree dikhaakar kaha ki kejariwal ne desh kaa naam badnaam kiya he

 pradhanmantri ne 1978 main tritiy shrenee main dilli vishvavidhyalay se bie paas kiya

 bijepi ne pradhanmantri kii marksheet bhi jari kii he, taaki aarope kii koi guzaaish na rahe

 pradhanmantri gujarat se dilli pariksha dene aate the

 aam aadmi party ne ise kaaphi gambhirtha se uthaaya he

 unhen aise skulon se bachanaa chahie jo bekaar kii degree ke naam par unhen gahare karz main daal dete hai
 Rajan said that we should see that unscrupulous schools do not target students who are not aware of them, because in such a situation they get stuck in debt along with a useless degree
 kai baar aapaki degree sahi hoti he lekin college hi farzi nikal jaataa he

 swami ke anusaar sonia gandhi ne 2004 ke halafname main apni degree ke bare main galat jaankaree di thi

 Swamy asked Cambridge University about Sonia Gandhi's degree, she was told that she had never been a student
 swami ne yah bhi aarope lagaaya tha ki sonia ne angrezi main jis certificate course kaa zikr kiya he, wo cambridge ke kisi bhi english teaching shop se mil saktaa he
 The Supreme Court dismissed Swamy's petition

 janata party ke netaa the

 jiesti council jiesti se jude sabhi ahm maamalon par faisla karegi

 Many times during pregnancy, you feel like eating anything and in such a situation, nothing should be eaten without the advice of the doctor, because eating anything like this can be harmful for both you and your child
 iske alaava bhi kuch healdi chijen bhi aapke liye nuksaandeh sabit ho sakati hai
 Let's know about 5 such healthy things which are beneficial for a normal human being but not for a pregnant woman
 
 
 1
 Raw egg eggs contain harmful organisms, e-coli and salmonella
 yahgarbhvatee mahila main aanton kaa infectionpaida kar saktaa he
 It is important to avoid the consumption of raw eggs during pregnancy
 2
 Soft cheese: Pregnant women should avoid eating soft cheese
 soft cheez main shaamil hai, phita, bri, or camembert paneer, blue veined cheez, cuso blonko, cuso fresco or funell
 This cheese may be safe to eat, but it has a pasteurized label
 3
 Unpasteurized milk and juice Unpasteurized milk and many soft cheese should be eaten during pregnancy
 agar cheez par yah label laga he ki vah poshcharide doodh se bana he to garbhavastha ke dauraan iskaa istemaal karnaa surakshit hai
 But if it is not clear from the label then it is better to avoid it because they may contain bacteria
 4
 Raw Sprouted Vegetables Raw sprouts should be avoided during pregnancy as bacteria are found during germination in such vegetables
 is prakaar ke kachche ankurit jaise alphala, tipatiyaa ghaas, muuli or mung khaane se bachein
 5
 herbal supplementamtaur par herbal supplement kii jaanch anya dawaaon kii tarah nahin hoti isliye ise garbhavastha ke dauraan surakshit nahin mana jaataa hai
 So before taking herbal supplements during pregnancy, you should talk to your doctor
